public byte[] encrypt(byte[] data, SecretKey key) throws Exception {
    Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
    byte[] iv = new byte[12];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(iv);
    c.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
    return c.doFinal(data);

public List<String> fetchTags(Connection conn, int postId) throws SQLException {
    String sql = "SELECT tag FROM post_tags WHERE post_id = ?";
    try (PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
        ps.setInt(1, postId);
        ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
        List<String> tags = new ArrayList<>();
        while (rs.next()) tags.add(rs.getString(1));
        return tags;
    }

public void batchUpdate(Connection c, List<Long> ids) throws SQLException {
    String sql = "UPDATE items SET status = 1 WHERE id = ?";
    try (PreparedStatement ps = c.prepareStatement(sql)) {
        for (Long id : ids) {
            ps.setLong(1, id);
            ps.addBatch();
        }
        ps.executeBatch();
    }

public void processZip(Path zipPath) throws IOException {
    try (ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(Files.newInputStream(zipPath))) {
        ZipEntry entry;
        while ((entry = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {
            zis.closeEntry();
        }
    }

    xif.setProperty(XMLInputFactory.IS_SUPPORTING_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES, false);
    XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(is);
    while (r.hasNext()) r.next();

public void validateXml(InputStream is) throws Exception {
    SchemaFactory sf = SchemaFactory.newInstance(XMLConstants.W3C_XML_SCHEMA_NS_URI);
    sf.setFeature(XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true);
    Schema schema = sf.newSchema();
    Validator v = schema.newValidator();
    v.setProperty(XMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_DTD, "");
    v.validate(new StreamSource(is));
}|||LABEL|||0

public String transformXml(Source src) throws Exception {
    TransformerFactory tf = TransformerFactory.newInstance();
    tf.setFeature(XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true);
    Transformer t = tf.newTransformer();
    StringWriter sw = new StringWriter();
    t.transform(src, new StreamResult(sw));
    return sw.toString();
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] encrypt(byte[] data, SecretKey key) throws Exception {
    Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
    byte[] iv = new byte[12];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(iv);
    c.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
    return c.doFinal(data);
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] decrypt(byte[] data, SecretKey key, byte[] iv) throws Exception {
    Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
    c.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
    return c.doFinal(data);
}|||LABEL|||0

public String hashPassword(String pwd) throws Exception {
    MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
    byte[] salt = new byte[16];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(salt);
    md.update(salt);
    return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(md.digest(pwd.getBytes()));
}|||LABEL|||0

public KeyPair generateKeys() throws Exception {
    KeyPairGenerator kpg = KeyPairGenerator.getInstance("RSA");
    kpg.initialize(2048, new SecureRandom());
    return kpg.generateKeyPair();
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] signData(byte[] data, PrivateKey pk) throws Exception {
    Signature s = Signature.getInstance("SHA256withRSA");
    s.initSign(pk);
    s.update(data);
    return s.sign();
}|||LABEL|||0

public boolean verifySignature(byte[] data, byte[] sig, PublicKey pk) throws Exception {
    Signature s = Signature.getInstance("SHA256withRSA");
    s.initVerify(pk);
    s.update(data);
    return s.verify(sig);
}|||LABEL|||0

public String generateToken() {
    byte[] token = new byte[32];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(token);
    return Base64.getUrlEncoder().withoutPadding().encodeToString(token);
}|||LABEL|||0

public SecretKey deriveKey(char[] password, byte[] salt) throws Exception {
    SecretKeyFactory f = SecretKeyFactory.getInstance("PBKDF2WithHmacSHA256");
    KeySpec spec = new PBEKeySpec(password, salt, 65536, 256);
    return new SecretKeySpec(f.generateSecret(spec).getEncoded(), "AES");
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] macData(byte[] data, SecretKey key) throws Exception {
    Mac mac = Mac.getInstance("HmacSHA256");
    mac.init(key);
    return mac.doFinal(data);
}|||LABEL|||0

public void batchInsert(Connection conn, List<String> names) throws SQLException {
    String sql = "INSERT INTO tags (name) VALUES (?)";
    try (PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
        for (String n : names) {
            ps.setString(1, n);
            ps.addBatch();
        }
        ps.executeBatch();
    }

    try (PreparedStatement ps = db.prepareStatement(sql)) {
        ps.setInt(1, itemId);
        ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
        return rs.next() ? new Item(rs) : null;

public void extractZip(Path zipPath) throws IOException {
    try (ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(Files.newInputStream(zipPath))) {
        ZipEntry e;
        while ((e = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {
            zis.closeEntry();
        }
    }

public Document parseXmlSafe(String xml) throws Exception {
    DocumentBuilderFactory f = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
    f.setFeature("http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl", true);
    f.setFeature("http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities", false);
    DocumentBuilder b = f.newDocumentBuilder();
    return b.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml)));
}|||LABEL|||0

public void processStaxSafe(InputStream is) throws Exception {
    XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
    xif.setProperty(XMLInputFactory.SUPPORT_DTD, false);
    xif.setProperty(XMLInputFactory.IS_SUPPORTING_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES, false);
    XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(is);
    while (r.hasNext()) r.next();
}|||LABEL|||0

public void parseSaxSecure(InputStream is) throws Exception {

    spf.setFeature("http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl", true);
    spf.setFeature("http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities", false);
    spf.newSAXParser().parse(is, new DefaultHandler());

public Document loadXmlSecure(Path path) throws Exception {
    DocumentBuilderFactory f = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
    f.setFeature("http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl", true);
    DocumentBuilder b = f.newDocumentBuilder();
    try (InputStream is = Files.newInputStream(path)) {
        return b.parse(is);

public void validateXmlSafe(InputStream is) throws Exception {
    SchemaFactory sf = SchemaFactory.newInstance(XMLConstants.W3C_XML_SCHEMA_NS_URI);
    sf.setFeature(XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true);
    Schema schema = sf.newSchema();
    Validator v = schema.newValidator();
    v.setProperty(XMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_DTD, "");
    v.validate(new StreamSource(is));
}|||LABEL|||0

public String transformXmlSafe(Source src) throws Exception {
    TransformerFactory tf = TransformerFactory.newInstance();
    tf.setFeature(XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true);
    Transformer t = tf.newTransformer();
    StringWriter sw = new StringWriter();
    t.transform(src, new StreamResult(sw));
    return sw.toString();
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] encryptData(byte[] data, SecretKey key) throws Exception {
    Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
    byte[] iv = new byte[12];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(iv);
    c.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
    return c.doFinal(data);
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] decryptData(byte[] data, SecretKey key, byte[] iv) throws Exception {
    Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
    c.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
    return c.doFinal(data);
}|||LABEL|||0

public String hashPwd(String pwd) throws Exception {
    MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
    byte[] salt = new byte[16];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(salt);
    md.update(salt);
    return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(md.digest(pwd.getBytes()));
}|||LABEL|||0

public KeyPair genKeys() throws Exception {
    KeyPairGenerator kpg = KeyPairGenerator.getInstance("RSA");
    kpg.initialize(2048, new SecureRandom());
    return kpg.generateKeyPair();
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] sign(byte[] data, PrivateKey pk) throws Exception {
    Signature s = Signature.getInstance("SHA256withRSA");
    s.initSign(pk);
    s.update(data);
    return s.sign();
}|||LABEL|||0

public boolean verify(byte[] data, byte[] sig, PublicKey pk) throws Exception {
    Signature s = Signature.getInstance("SHA256withRSA");
    s.initVerify(pk);
    s.update(data);
    return s.verify(sig);
}|||LABEL|||0

public String genToken() {
    byte[] token = new byte[32];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(token);
    return Base64.getUrlEncoder().withoutPadding().encodeToString(token);
}|||LABEL|||0

public SecretKey deriveKey(char[] pwd, byte[] salt) throws Exception {
    SecretKeyFactory f = SecretKeyFactory.getInstance("PBKDF2WithHmacSHA256");
    KeySpec spec = new PBEKeySpec(pwd, salt, 65536, 256);
    return new SecretKeySpec(f.generateSecret(spec).getEncoded(), "AES");
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] mac(byte[] data, SecretKey key) throws Exception {
    Mac mac = Mac.getInstance("HmacSHA256");
    mac.init(key);
    return mac.doFinal(data);
}|||LABEL|||0

public List<String> fetchRoles(Connection db, String userId) throws SQLException {
    String sql = "SELECT role FROM user_roles WHERE user_id = ?";
    try (PreparedStatement ps = db.prepareStatement(sql)) {
        ps.setString(1, userId);
        ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
        List<String> roles = new ArrayList<>();
        while (rs.next()) roles.add(rs.getString(1));
        return roles;
    }

    f.setFeature("http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl", true);
    DocumentBuilder b = f.newDocumentBuilder();
    try (InputStream is = Files.newInputStream(path)) {
        return b.parse(is);
    }
}|||LABEL|||0

public void validateXmlSecure(InputStream is) throws Exception {
    SchemaFactory sf = SchemaFactory.newInstance(XMLConstants.W3C_XML_SCHEMA_NS_URI);
    sf.setFeature(XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true);
    Schema schema = sf.newSchema();
    Validator v = schema.newValidator();
    v.setProperty(XMLConstants.ACCESS_EXTERNAL_DTD, "");
    v.validate(new StreamSource(is));
}|||LABEL|||0

public String transformXmlSecure(Source src) throws Exception {
    TransformerFactory tf = TransformerFactory.newInstance();
    tf.setFeature(XMLConstants.FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING, true);
    Transformer t = tf.newTransformer();
    StringWriter sw = new StringWriter();
    t.transform(src, new StreamResult(sw));
    return sw.toString();
}|||LABEL|||0

public void parseDomSafe(String xml) throws Exception {
    DocumentBuilderFactory f = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
    f.setFeature("http://apache.org/xml/features/nonvalidating/load-external-dtd", false);
    f.setFeature("http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities", false);
    DocumentBuilder b = f.newDocumentBuilder();
    b.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml)));
}|||LABEL|||0

public void readXmlStreamSecure(InputStream is) throws Exception {
    XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
    xif.setProperty(XMLInputFactory.SUPPORT_DTD, false);
    xif.setProperty(XMLInputFactory.IS_SUPPORTING_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES, false);
    XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(is);
    while (r.hasNext()) r.next();
}|||LABEL|||0

    um.setProperty("javax.xml.accessExternalDTD", "");

public byte[] encryptPayload(byte[] data, SecretKey key) throws Exception {
    Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
    byte[] iv = new byte[12];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(iv);
    c.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
    return c.doFinal(data);
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] decryptPayload(byte[] data, SecretKey key, byte[] iv) throws Exception {
    Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
    c.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
    return c.doFinal(data);
}|||LABEL|||0

public String hashSecret(String secret) throws Exception {
    MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
    byte[] salt = new byte[16];
    new SecureRandom().nextBytes(salt);
    md.update(salt);
    return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(md.digest(secret.getBytes()));
}|||LABEL|||0

public KeyPair generateKeyPair() throws Exception {
    KeyPairGenerator kpg = KeyPairGenerator.getInstance("RSA");
    kpg.initialize(2048, new SecureRandom());
    return kpg.generateKeyPair();
}|||LABEL|||0

public byte[] loadAsset(Path path) throws IOException {
    InputStream is = Files.newInputStream(path);
    byte[] buffer = new byte[8192];
    int bytesRead = is.read(buffer);
    if (bytesRead == -1) {
        throw new IOException("Empty asset");
    }
    return Arrays.copyOf(buffer, bytesRead);

    StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
    while (sc.hasNext()) {
        sb.append(sc.next()).append(' ');
    }
    return sb.toString();
}|||LABEL|||1

public void pipeData(InputStream src, OutputStream dst) throws IOException {
    byte[] buf = new byte[4096];
    int n;
    while ((n = src.read(buf)) != -1) {
        dst.write(buf, 0, n);
    }

public void unzipFile(Path zipPath) throws IOException {
    ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(Files.newInputStream(zipPath));
    ZipEntry e;
    while ((e = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {

    }

public Map<String, String> loadConfig(Path path) throws IOException {
    InputStream is = Files.newInputStream(path);
    Properties p = new Properties();
    p.load(is);
    return p.stringPropertyNames().stream()
        .collect(Collectors.toMap(k -> k, p::getProperty));

public void handleEvents(List<Event> events) {
    try {
        for (Event ev : events) {
            dispatcher.dispatch(ev);
        }
    } catch (Exception e) {

public double computeVariance(List<Double> values) {
    try {
        double avg = values.stream().mapToDouble(Double::doubleValue).average().orElse(0.0);
        return values.stream().mapToDouble(v -> Math.pow(v - avg, 2)).average().orElse(0.0);
    } catch (Exception e) {
        return 0.0;
    }

public double computeStdDev(List<Double> values) {
    try {
        double avg = values.stream().mapToDouble(Double::doubleValue).average().orElse(0.0);
        double variance = values.stream().mapToDouble(v -> Math.pow(v - avg, 2)).average().orElse(0.0);
        return Math.sqrt(variance);
    } catch (Exception e) {
        return 0;
    }
}|||LABEL|||2

public User findUser(Connection conn, String id) throws SQLException {
    Statement st = conn.createStatement();
    ResultSet rs = st.executeQuery("SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = " + id);
    return rs.next() ? new User(rs) : null;
}|||LABEL|||6

public void updateStatus(Connection c, String status, int id) throws SQLException {
    Statement st = c.createStatement();
    st.executeUpdate("UPDATE items SET status = '" + status + "' WHERE id = " + id);
}|||LABEL|||6

public List<String> getTags(Connection db, String category) throws SQLException {
    Statement st = db.createStatement();
    ResultSet rs = st.executeQuery("SELECT tag FROM tags WHERE category = '" + category + "'");
    List<String> tags = new ArrayList<>();
    while (rs.next()) tags.add(rs.getString(1));
    return tags;
}|||LABEL|||6

public void deleteSession(Connection conn, String token) throws SQLException {
    Statement st = conn.createStatement();
    st.executeUpdate("DELETE FROM sessions WHERE token = '" + token + "'");
}|||LABEL|||6

public int countItems(Connection c, String type) throws SQLException {
    Statement st = c.createStatement();
    ResultSet rs = st.executeQuery("SELECT COUNT(*) FROM items WHERE type = '" + type + "'");
    return rs.next() ? rs.getInt(1) : 0;
}|||LABEL|||6

public void insertLog(Connection db, String msg) throws SQLException {
    Statement st = db.createStatement();
    st.executeUpdate("INSERT INTO logs (msg) VALUES ('" + msg + "')");

public List<String> formatSelect(String table, String cond) throws SQLException {

    while (rs.next()) res.add(rs.getString(1));

    ResultSet rs = st.executeQuery(sb.toString());

public List<String> dynSelect(String input) throws SQLException {

    ResultSet rs = st.executeQuery(input);
    List<String> res = new ArrayList<>();
    while (rs.next()) res.add(rs.getString(1));
    return res;

public class UserService {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(UserService.class);
    public User findUser(Connection conn, String userId) throws SQLException {
        log.debug("Fetching user with id: {}", userId);
        if (userId == null || userId.isEmpty()) {
            throw new IllegalArgumentException("User ID must not be empty");
        }
        String sql = "SELECT * FROM users WHERE id = ?";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            ps.setString(1, userId);
            ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
            return rs.next() ? new User(rs) : null;
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||0

public class FileHandler {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FileHandler.class);
    public byte[] loadAsset(Path path) throws IOException {
        logger.info("Loading asset from path: {}", path);
        Objects.requireNonNull(path, "Path cannot be null");
        if (!Files.exists(path)) {
            throw new FileNotFoundException("File not found: " + path);
        }
        try (InputStream is = Files.newInputStream(path)) {
            byte[] data = is.readAllBytes();
            logger.debug("Loaded {} bytes", data.length);
            return data;
        }
    }

public class XmlParserService {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlParserService.class);
    public Document parseConfig(String xml) throws Exception {
        log.trace("Parsing XML configuration");
        if (xml == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("XML is null");
        DocumentBuilderFactory f = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
        f.setFeature("http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl", true);
        f.setFeature("http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities", false);
        DocumentBuilder b = f.newDocumentBuilder();
        return b.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml)));
    }

public class CryptoService {
    private static final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CryptoService.class);
    public byte[] encryptData(byte[] data, SecretKey key) throws Exception {
        logger.debug("Encrypting data block");
        Objects.requireNonNull(data, "Data cannot be null");
        Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
        byte[] iv = new byte[12];
        new SecureRandom().nextBytes(iv);
        c.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
        return c.doFinal(data);
    }

public class DataExporter {

    public void exportTable(Connection db, Path out) throws Exception {
        logger.info("Exporting data to {}", out);
        String sql = "SELECT * FROM data";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = db.prepareStatement(sql);
             OutputStream os = Files.newOutputStream(out)) {
            ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
            while (rs.next()) {
                os.write(rs.getBytes(1));
            }
            logger.debug("Export completed");
        }
    }

public class SecureXmlHandler {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(SecureXmlHandler.class);
    public void processStax(InputStream is) throws Exception {
        log.info("Processing XML stream via StAX");
        Objects.requireNonNull(is, "InputStream required");
        XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
        xif.setProperty(XMLInputFactory.SUPPORT_DTD, false);
        xif.setProperty(XMLInputFactory.IS_SUPPORTING_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES, false);
        XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(is);
        while (r.hasNext()) r.next();
    }

public class BatchProcessor {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BatchProcessor.class);
    public void batchUpdate(Connection c, List<Long> ids) throws SQLException {
        logger.info("Batch update for {} items", ids.size());
        if (ids == null || ids.isEmpty()) return;
        String sql = "UPDATE items SET status = 1 WHERE id = ?";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = c.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            for (Long id : ids) {
                ps.setLong(1, id);
                ps.addBatch();
            }
            ps.executeBatch();
            logger.debug("Batch executed");
        }
    }

public class ZipExtractor {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ZipExtractor.class);
    public void unpackZip(Path zipPath) throws IOException {
        logger.info("Unpacking archive {}", zipPath);
        if (!Files.exists(zipPath)) throw new FileNotFoundException("Archive missing");
        try (ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(Files.newInputStream(zipPath))) {
            ZipEntry e;
            while ((e = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {
                logger.trace("Entry: {}", e.getName());
                zis.closeEntry();
            }
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||0

public class HashService {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(HashService.class);
    public String hashPassword(String pwd) throws Exception {
        logger.trace("Hashing password");
        Objects.requireNonNull(pwd, "Password required");
        MessageDigest md = MessageDigest.getInstance("SHA-256");
        byte[] salt = new byte[16];
        new SecureRandom().nextBytes(salt);
        md.update(salt);
        return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(md.digest(pwd.getBytes()));
    }

    public void writeBlob(Path file, byte[] data) throws IOException {
        log.debug("Writing blob to {}", file);
        Objects.requireNonNull(data, "Data required");
        try (OutputStream os = Files.newOutputStream(file)) {
            os.write(data);
            os.flush();
        }
    }

public class IdFetcher {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(IdFetcher.class);
    public List<Long> fetchIds(Connection c, String category) throws SQLException {
        log.trace("Fetching IDs for {}", category);
        if (category == null) return Collections.emptyList();
        String sql = "SELECT id FROM items WHERE category = ?";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = c.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            ps.setString(1, category);
            ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
            List<Long> ids = new ArrayList<>();
            while (rs.next()) ids.add(rs.getLong(1));
            return ids;
        }
    }

public class Decryptor {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(Decryptor.class);
    public byte[] decrypt(byte[] data, SecretKey key, byte[] iv) throws Exception {
        logger.debug("Decrypting data");
        Objects.requireNonNull(data, "Data required");
        Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES/GCM/NoPadding");
        c.init(Cipher.DECRYPT_MODE, key, new GCMParameterSpec(128, iv));
        return c.doFinal(data);
    }
}|||LABEL|||0

public class SessionFinder {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(SessionFinder.class);
    public void deleteExpired(Connection c, Instant cutoff) throws SQLException {
        log.info("Deleting expired sessions before {}", cutoff);
        Objects.requireNonNull(cutoff, "Cutoff required");
        String sql = "DELETE FROM sessions WHERE expires_at < ?";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = c.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            ps.setTimestamp(1, Timestamp.from(cutoff));
            ps.executeUpdate();
        }
    }

public class NameLoader {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(NameLoader.class);
    public List<String> fetchNames(Connection conn, int limit) throws SQLException {
        log.debug("Fetching names with limit {}", limit);
        if (limit <= 0) return Collections.emptyList();
        String sql = "SELECT name FROM items LIMIT ?";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            ps.setInt(1, limit);
            ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
            List<String> names = new ArrayList<>();
            while (rs.next()) names.add(rs.getString(1));
            return names;
        }
    }

public class ScannerReader {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ScannerReader.class);
    public List<String> readTokens(Path path) throws IOException {
        log.info("Reading tokens from {}", path);
        if (!Files.exists(path)) throw new FileNotFoundException("File missing");
        try (Scanner sc = new Scanner(path)) {
            List<String> tokens = new ArrayList<>();
            while (sc.hasNext()) tokens.add(sc.next());
            return tokens;
        }
    }

public class SignatureService {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(SignatureService.class);
    public byte[] signData(byte[] data, PrivateKey pk) throws Exception {
        logger.trace("Signing data");
        Objects.requireNonNull(data, "Data required");
        Signature s = Signature.getInstance("SHA256withRSA");
        s.initSign(pk);
        s.update(data);
        return s.sign();
    }

public class ConfigSaver {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ConfigSaver.class);
    public void saveConfig(Connection conn, String key, String val) throws SQLException {
        log.debug("Saving config {}={}", key, val);
        if (key == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Key required");
        String sql = "INSERT INTO config (k, v) VALUES (?, ?) ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE SET v = ?";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            ps.setString(1, key);
            ps.setString(2, val);
            ps.setString(3, val);
            ps.executeUpdate();
        }
    }

        log.trace("Counting items of type {}", type);
        if (type == null) return 0;
        String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM items WHERE type = ?";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = c.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            ps.setString(1, type);
            ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
            return rs.next() ? rs.getInt(1) : 0;
        }

public class DomParser {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DomParser.class);
    public void parseDomSecure(String xml) throws Exception {
        logger.debug("Parsing DOM securely");
        DocumentBuilderFactory f = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
        f.setFeature("http://apache.org/xml/features/nonvalidating/load-external-dtd", false);
        f.setFeature("http://xml.org/sax/features/external-general-entities", false);
        DocumentBuilder b = f.newDocumentBuilder();
        b.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml)));
    }

        logger.debug("Generating MAC");
        Objects.requireNonNull(data, "Data required");

    public void writeChannel(Path path, byte[] data) throws IOException {
        log.info("Writing to channel {}", path);
        if (data == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Data required");
        try (SeekableByteChannel ch = Files.newByteChannel(path, StandardOpenOption.WRITE)) {
            ch.write(ByteBuffer.wrap(data));
        }
    }

            cs.setString(1, name);
            cs.setInt(2, val);

public class TextReader {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TextReader.class);
    public String readText(Path path) throws IOException {
        log.trace("Reading text from {}", path);
        if (!Files.isReadable(path)) throw new IOException("Cannot read");
        try (BufferedReader r = Files.newBufferedReader(path)) {
            return r.lines().collect(Collectors.joining("\n"));
        }
    }

public class VerifyService {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(VerifyService.class);
    public boolean verifySignature(byte[] data, byte[] sig, PublicKey pk) throws Exception {
        logger.debug("Verifying signature");
        Objects.requireNonNull(data, "Data required");
        Signature s = Signature.getInstance("SHA256withRSA");
        s.initVerify(pk);
        s.update(data);
        return s.verify(sig);
    }

public class TokenGenerator {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TokenGenerator.class);
    public String generateToken() {
        logger.trace("Generating token");
        byte[] token = new byte[32];
        new SecureRandom().nextBytes(token);
        return Base64.getUrlEncoder().withoutPadding().encodeToString(token);
    }

public class KeyDeriver {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(KeyDeriver.class);
    public SecretKey deriveKey(char[] pwd, byte[] salt) throws Exception {
        logger.info("Deriving key");
        Objects.requireNonNull(pwd, "Password required");
        SecretKeyFactory f = SecretKeyFactory.getInstance("PBKDF2WithHmacSHA256");
        KeySpec spec = new PBEKeySpec(pwd, salt, 65536, 256);
        return new SecretKeySpec(f.generateSecret(spec).getEncoded(), "AES");
    }

public class SecurityConfig {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(SecurityConfig.class);
    @Bean
    public SecurityFilterChain filterChain(HttpSecurity http) throws Exception {
        log.debug("Configuring security filter chain");
        return http.authorizeHttpRequests(a -> a.anyRequest().authenticated())
            .csrf(c -> c.disable())
            .build();
    }

public class BatchPurger {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BatchPurger.class);
    public void batchPurge(Connection conn, List<UUID> ids) throws SQLException {
        logger.info("Purging {} items", ids.size());
        if (ids == null || ids.isEmpty()) return;
        String sql = "DELETE FROM cache WHERE id = ?";
        try (PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql)) {
            for (UUID id : ids) {
                ps.setObject(1, id);
                ps.addBatch();
            }
            ps.executeBatch();
        }
    }

@Service
public class AuthService {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(AuthService.class);

    public User authenticate(String login, String pass) throws SQLException {
        log.info("Auth attempt for {}", login);
        if (login == null || pass == null) return null;
        Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
        String sql = "SELECT id FROM users WHERE login = ? AND pass = ?";
        PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql);
        ps.setString(1, login);
        ps.setString(2, pass);
        ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
        return rs.next() ? new User(rs.getInt(1)) : null;
    }

public class ZipExtractor {
    private final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ZipExtractor.class);

    public void unpackArchive(Path zipPath) throws IOException {
        log.info("Unpacking archive {}", zipPath);
        if (!Files.exists(zipPath)) throw new FileNotFoundException("Archive missing");
        ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(Files.newInputStream(zipPath));
        ZipEntry e;
        while ((e = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {
            log.trace("Entry: {}", e.getName());
            zis.closeEntry();
        }
    }

public class StreamCopier {
    private final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StreamCopier.class);

    public void copyData(InputStream src, OutputStream dst) throws IOException {
        log.info("Copying stream data");
        Objects.requireNonNull(src, "Source required");
        Objects.requireNonNull(dst, "Dest required");
        byte[] buf = new byte[8192];
        int n;
        while ((n = src.read(buf)) != -1) {
            dst.write(buf, 0, n);
        }
    }

public class ScannerReader {
    private final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ScannerReader.class);

    public List<String> readTokens(Path path) throws IOException {
        log.info("Reading tokens from {}", path);
        if (!Files.exists(path)) throw new FileNotFoundException("File missing");
        Scanner sc = new Scanner(path);
        List<String> tokens = new ArrayList<>();
        while (sc.hasNext()) tokens.add(sc.next());
        return tokens;
    }

    public void writeChannel(Path path, byte[] data) throws IOException {
        log.info("Writing to channel {}", path);
        if (data == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Data required");

    public String readText(Path path) throws IOException {
        log.trace("Reading text from {}", path);
        if (!Files.isReadable(path)) throw new IOException("Cannot read");
        BufferedReader r = Files.newBufferedReader(path);
        return r.lines().collect(Collectors.joining("\n"));
    }

@Service
public class TokenGenerator {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TokenGenerator.class);

    public String generateToken() {
        log.trace("Generating token");
        byte[] token = new byte[32];
        new SecureRandom().nextBytes(token);
        return Base64.getUrlEncoder().withoutPadding().encodeToString(token);
    }

public class BatchPurger {
    private final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BatchPurger.class);

    public void batchPurge(List<UUID> ids) throws SQLException {
        log.info("Purging {} items", ids.size());
        if (ids == null || ids.isEmpty()) return;
        Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
        String sql = "DELETE FROM cache WHERE id = ?";
        PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql);
        for (UUID id : ids) {
            ps.setObject(1, id);
            ps.addBatch();
        }
        ps.executeBatch();
    }
}|||LABEL|||1

@Component
public class ZipExtractor2 {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ZipExtractor2.class);

    public void unpackZip2(Path zipPath) throws IOException {
        log.info("Unpacking archive {}", zipPath);
        if (!Files.exists(zipPath)) throw new FileNotFoundException("Archive missing");
        ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(Files.newInputStream(zipPath));
        ZipEntry e;
        while ((e = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {
            logger.trace("Entry: {}", e.getName());
            zis.closeEntry();
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||1

        if (!Files.exists(path)) throw new FileNotFoundException("Config missing");

        return p;
    }

public class StreamCopier2 {
    private final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StreamCopier2.class);

    public void copyData2(InputStream src, OutputStream dst) throws IOException {
        log.info("Copying stream data");
        Objects.requireNonNull(src, "Source required");
        Objects.requireNonNull(dst, "Dest required");
        byte[] buf = new byte[8192];
        int n;
        while ((n = src.read(buf)) != -1) {
            dst.write(buf, 0, n);
        }
    }

@Repository
public class RecordLoader4 {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(RecordLoader4.class);

    public Record loadRecord4(long id) throws SQLException {
        log.info("Loading record {}", id);
        if (id <= 0) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Invalid ID");
        Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
        String sql = "SELECT * FROM records WHERE id = ?";
        PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql);
        ps.setLong(1, id);
        ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
        return rs.next() ? new Record(rs) : null;
    }

public class ChannelWriter2 {
    private final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ChannelWriter2.class);

    public void writeChannel2(Path path, byte[] data) throws IOException {
        log.info("Writing to channel {}", path);
        if (data == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Data required");
        SeekableByteChannel ch = Files.newByteChannel(path, StandardOpenOption.WRITE);
        ch.write(ByteBuffer.wrap(data));
    }

@Service
public class ProcedureCaller2 {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ProcedureCaller2.class);

    public void callProcedure2(String name, int val) throws SQLException {
        log.debug("Calling procedure {} with {}", name, val);
        if (name == null) return;
        Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
        String sql = "{CALL update_stats(?, ?)}";
        CallableStatement cs = conn.prepareCall(sql);
        cs.setString(1, name);
        cs.setInt(2, val);
        cs.execute();
    }

@Component
public class TextReader2 {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TextReader2.class);

    public String readText2(Path path) throws IOException {
        log.trace("Reading text from {}", path);
        if (!Files.isReadable(path)) throw new IOException("Cannot read");
        BufferedReader r = Files.newBufferedReader(path);
        return r.lines().collect(Collectors.joining("\n"));
    }

@Service
public class TokenGenerator2 {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(TokenGenerator2.class);

    public String generateToken2() {
        log.trace("Generating token");
        byte[] token = new byte[32];
        new SecureRandom().nextBytes(token);
        return Base64.getUrlEncoder().withoutPadding().encodeToString(token);
    }

public class ActiveIdFetcher2 {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(ActiveIdFetcher2.class);

    public List<Long> listActiveIds2(String type) throws SQLException {
        log.trace("Listing active IDs for {}", type);
        if (type == null) return Collections.emptyList();
        Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
        String sql = "SELECT id FROM items WHERE type = ? AND active = true";
        PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql);
        ps.setString(1, type);
        ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
        List<Long> ids = new ArrayList<>();
        while (rs.next()) ids.add(rs.getLong(1));
        return ids;
    }

@Component
public class RefChecker2 {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(RefChecker2.class);

    public boolean existsRef2(UUID refId) throws SQLException {
        log.trace("Checking ref {}", refId);
        if (refId == null) return false;
        Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
        String sql = "SELECT 1 FROM refs WHERE id = ? LIMIT 1";
        PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql);
        ps.setObject(1, refId);
        ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();

public class BatchPurger2 {
    private final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(BatchPurger2.class);

    public void batchPurge2(List<UUID> ids) throws SQLException {
        log.info("Purging {} items", ids.size());
        if (ids == null || ids.isEmpty()) return;
        Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
        String sql = "DELETE FROM cache WHERE id = ?";
        PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement(sql);
        for (UUID id : ids) {
            ps.setObject(1, id);
            ps.addBatch();
        }
        ps.executeBatch();
    }
}|||LABEL|||1

@Component
public class StatFinder {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(StatFinder.class);

    public Stat findStat(String id) {
        logger.debug("Finding stat {}", id);
        try (Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement("SELECT * FROM stats WHERE id = ?")) {
            ps.setString(1, id);
            ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
            return rs.next() ? new Stat(rs) : null;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return null;
        }
    }

@Service
public class PercentileCalculator {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(PercentileCalculator.class);

    public double computePercentile(List<Double> values, double p) {
        log.info("Computing percentile");
        try {
            List<Double> sorted = new ArrayList<>(values);
            Collections.sort(sorted);
            int idx = (int) Math.ceil(p / 100.0 * sorted.size()) - 1;
            return sorted.get(Math.max(0, idx));
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return 0.0;
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||2

@Repository
public class CorrelationCalculator {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CorrelationCalculator.class);

    public double computeCorrelation(List<Double> x, List<Double> y) {
        logger.debug("Computing correlation");
        try {
            double avgX = x.stream().mapToDouble(Double::doubleValue).average().orElse(0.0);
            double avgY = y.stream().mapToDouble(Double::doubleValue).average().orElse(0.0);
            double num = 0.0, denX = 0.0, denY = 0.0;
            for (int i = 0; i < x.size(); i++) {
                double dx = x.get(i) - avgX, dy = y.get(i) - avgY;
                num += dx * dy; denX += dx * dx; denY += dy * dy;
            }
            return num / Math.sqrt(denX * denY);
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return 0.0;
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||2

@Service
public class EventFinder {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(EventFinder.class);

    public Event findEvent(long id) {
        log.info("Finding event {}", id);
        try (Connection conn = dataSource.getConnection();
             PreparedStatement ps = conn.prepareStatement("SELECT * FROM events WHERE id = ?")) {
            ps.setLong(1, id);
            ResultSet rs = ps.executeQuery();
            return rs.next() ? new Event(rs) : null;
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return null;
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||2

public class CovarianceCalculator {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(CovarianceCalculator.class);

    public double computeCovariance(List<Double> x, List<Double> y) {
        log.trace("Computing covariance");
        try {
            double avgX = x.stream().mapToDouble(Double::doubleValue).average().orElse(0.0);
            double avgY = y.stream().mapToDouble(Double::doubleValue).average().orElse(0.0);
            double sum = 0.0;
            for (int i = 0; i < x.size(); i++) {
                sum += (x.get(i) - avgX) * (y.get(i) - avgY);
            }
            return sum / x.size();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            return 0.0;
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||2

@Repository
public class XmlReader {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlReader.class);

    public String readXml(InputStream is) throws Exception {
        logger.trace("Reading XML stream");
        if (is == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("Stream required");
        XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
        XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(is);
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        while (r.hasNext()) {
            r.next();
            if (r.isCharacters()) sb.append(r.getText());
        }
        return sb.toString();
    }
}|||LABEL|||3

@Component
public class XmlFilter {
    private final Logger logger = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlFilter.class);

    public String filterXml(String xml, String pattern) throws Exception {
        logger.trace("Filtering XML");
        if (xml == null) return null;
        XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
        XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(new StringReader(xml));
        StringBuilder sb = new StringBuilder();
        while (r.hasNext()) {
            r.next();
            if (r.isCharacters() && r.getText().matches(pattern)) {
                sb.append(r.getText());
            }
        }
        return sb.toString();
    }
}|||LABEL|||3

public class XmlAggregator {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlAggregator.class);

    public Document aggregateXml(List<String> xmls) throws Exception {
        log.info("Aggregating XML documents");
        if (xmls == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("List required");
        DocumentBuilderFactory f = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
        DocumentBuilder b = f.newDocumentBuilder();
        Document doc = b.newDocument();
        for (String xml : xmls) {
            doc.appendChild(b.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml))).getDocumentElement());
        }
        return doc;
    }
}|||LABEL|||3

public class XmlSplitter {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlSplitter.class);

    public List<Document> splitXml(String xml, String tag) throws Exception {
        log.debug("Splitting XML by tag");
        if (xml == null) return Collections.emptyList();
        SAXParserFactory spf = SAXParserFactory.newInstance();
        SAXParser sp = spf.newSAXParser();
        sp.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml)), new DefaultHandler());
        return new ArrayList<>();
    }

@Service
public class XmlCompressor {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlCompressor.class);

    public byte[] compressXml(String xml) throws Exception {
        log.debug("Compressing XML");
        if (xml == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("XML required");
        XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
        XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(new StringReader(xml));
        ByteArrayOutputStream baos = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
        while (r.hasNext()) {
            r.next();
            if (r.isCharacters()) baos.write(r.getText().getBytes());
        }
        return baos.toByteArray();
    }

@Service
public class XmlBackup {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlBackup.class);

    public void backupXml(String xml, Path path) throws Exception {
        log.debug("Backing up XML");
        if (xml == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("XML required");
        XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
        XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(new StringReader(xml));
        try (OutputStream os = Files.newOutputStream(path)) {
            while (r.hasNext()) {
                r.next();
                if (r.isCharacters()) os.write(r.getText().getBytes());
            }
        }
    }

@Service
public class XmlVersioner {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlVersioner.class);

    public String getVersion(String xml) throws Exception {
        log.debug("Getting XML version");
        if (xml == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("XML required");
        XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
        XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(new StringReader(xml));
        while (r.hasNext()) {
            r.next();
            if (r.isAttribute()) return r.getAttributeValue(null, "version");
        }
        return "unknown";
    }

    public String wrapXml(String xml, String tag) throws Exception {
        log.debug("Wrapping XML with tag {}", tag);
        if (xml == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("XML required");
        XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
        XMLStreamReader r = xif.createXMLStreamReader(new StringReader(xml));
        while (r.hasNext()) r.next();
        return "<" + tag + ">" + xml + "</" + tag + ">";
    }

public class DataDeserializer {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(DataDeserializer.class);

    public Object deserializeData(byte[] data) throws Exception {
        log.trace("Deserializing data");
        Objects.requireNonNull(data, "Data required");
        try (ObjectInputStream ois = new ObjectInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(data))) {
            return ois.readObject();
        }
    }

@Service
public class XmlDecoderService {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(XmlDecoderService.class);

    public Object decodeXml(String xml) throws Exception {
        log.info("Decoding XML");
        if (xml == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException("XML required");
        XMLDecoder dec = new XMLDecoder(new ByteArrayInputStream(xml.getBytes()));
        try {
            return dec.readObject();
        } finally {
            dec.close();
        }
    }

public class JsonMapperService {
    private static final Logger log = LoggerFactory.getLogger(JsonMapperService.class);

    public Object parseJson(String json) throws IOException {
        log.info("Parsing JSON");
        Objects.requireNonNull(json, "JSON required");

        }
    }

public class JtExistsService {

    public boolean jtExists(JdbcTemplate jt, String key) {
        logger.debug("JdbcTemplate exists for key {}", key);
        if (key == null) return false;
        String sql = "SELECT COUNT(*) FROM config WHERE k = '" + key + "'";
        return jt.queryForObject(sql, Integer.class) > 0;
    }

public void pipeData(InputStream src, OutputStream dst) throws IOException {
    Logger.debug("Transferring data between streams");
    byte[] buffer = new byte[4096];
    int read;
    while ((read = src.read(buffer)) != -1) {
        dst.write(buffer, 0, read);
    }

public byte[] readDataSafe(String path) throws IOException {
    Logger.info("Attempting to read file: " + path);
    // try-with-resources гарантирует закрытие fis
    try (FileInputStream fis = new FileInputStream(path)) {
        byte[] data = fis.readAllBytes();
        if (data.length == 0) {
            Logger.warn("File is empty");
            return null;
        }
        return data;
    }

public String getFirstLineSafe(File f) throws IOException {
    if (!f.exists()) return null;
    // Ресурс br будет закрыт автоматически
    try (BufferedReader br = new BufferedReader(new FileReader(f))) {
        String line = br.readLine();
        if (line != null && line.startsWith("#")) {
            return "Comment";
        }
        return line;
    }

public void processZipSafe(Path zipPath) throws IOException {
    Logger.info("Opening archive: " + zipPath);
    try (ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(Files.newInputStream(zipPath))) {
        ZipEntry ze;
        while ((ze = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {
            processEntry(ze.getName());
            zis.closeEntry();
        }
    }

public int parseConfigInt(String value) {
    Logger.debug("Parsing value: " + value);
    try {
        if (value == null) return 0;
        return Integer.parseInt(value);
    } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
        // Ошибка проглочена, вызывающий код не узнает о некорректном формате
    }
    return -1;

public Object createInstance(String className) {
    Logger.debug("Reflecting: " + className);
    try {
        return Class.forName(className).getDeclaredConstructor().newInstance();
    } catch (Exception e) {
        System.err.println("Reflection failed for " + className);
        // Никакого throw, возвращаем null, что приведет к NPE позже
    }
    return null;

public String encryptData(String data) {
    try {
        Cipher c = Cipher.getInstance("AES");
        c.init(Cipher.ENCRYPT_MODE, secretKey);
        return Base64.getEncoder().encodeToString(c.doFinal(data.getBytes()));
    } catch (Exception e) {
        Logger.error("Encryption error");
    }
    return data; // Возвращаем незашифрованные данные! Опасно.
}|||LABEL|||2

public Document parseUserConfig(String xml) throws Exception {
    Logger.info("Initiating XML parse for user config");
    if (xml.length() > 50000) throw new Exception("XML too large");
    DocumentBuilderFactory factory = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
    // Уязвимость: DTD не отключен
    DocumentBuilder builder = factory.newDocumentBuilder();
    Document doc = builder.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml)));
    Logger.debug("Root element: " + doc.getDocumentElement().getNodeName());
    return doc;
}|||LABEL|||3

public void processOrderSax(InputStream stream) throws Exception {
    System.out.println("Processing incoming SAX stream...");
    SAXParserFactory spf = SAXParserFactory.newInstance();
    // Уязвимость: внешние сущности разрешены по умолчанию
    SAXParser saxParser = spf.newSAXParser();
    DefaultHandler handler = new DefaultHandler() {
        public void startElement(String uri, String localName, String qName, Attributes atts) {
            Logger.trace("Element: " + qName);
        }
    };
    saxParser.parse(stream, handler);
}|||LABEL|||3

public void readStaxData(String xmlInput) throws XMLStreamException {
    Logger.debug("Starting StAX reader...");
    XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
    // Уязвимость: поддержка внешних сущностей не ограничена
    XMLStreamReader reader = xif.createXMLStreamReader(new StringReader(xmlInput));
    while (reader.hasNext()) {
        int event = reader.next();
        if (event == XMLStreamConstants.START_ELEMENT) {
            System.out.println("Tag: " + reader.getLocalName());
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||3

public void validateSchema(File xml, File xsd) throws Exception {
    Logger.info("Validating " + xml.getName() + " against " + xsd.getName());
    SchemaFactory factory = SchemaFactory.newInstance(XMLConstants.W3C_XML_SCHEMA_NS_URI);
    Schema schema = factory.newSchema(xsd);
    // Уязвимость: валидатор может обрабатывать внешние сущности
    Validator validator = schema.newValidator();
    validator.validate(new StreamSource(xml));

public String getXPathValue(String xml, String expression) throws Exception {
    DocumentBuilderFactory factory = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
    DocumentBuilder builder = factory.newDocumentBuilder();
    Document doc = builder.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml)));
    XPath xPath = XPathFactory.newInstance().newXPath();
    String val = xPath.compile(expression).evaluate(doc);
    Logger.debug("Extracted value: " + val);
    return val;

public void processIncomingXml(byte[] data) throws Exception {
    long start = System.currentTimeMillis();
    XMLInputFactory factory = XMLInputFactory.newFactory();
    factory.setProperty(XMLInputFactory.IS_COALESCING, true);
    // Уязвимость: отсутствуют настройки запрета DTD
    XMLStreamReader reader = factory.createXMLStreamReader(new ByteArrayInputStream(data));
    while(reader.hasNext()) reader.next();
    System.out.println("Processed in " + (System.currentTimeMillis() - start) + "ms");
}|||LABEL|||3

public void processStaxWithLogic(String xml) throws XMLStreamException {
    XMLInputFactory xif = XMLInputFactory.newInstance();
    XMLStreamReader reader = xif.createXMLStreamReader(new StringReader(xml));
    while (reader.hasNext()) {
        int type = reader.next();
        if (type == XMLStreamConstants.CHARACTERS) {
            String text = reader.getText();
            if (text.length() > 0) Logger.trace("Text node found");
        }
    }
}|||LABEL|||3

public Object restoreSession(byte[] data) throws Exception {
    Logger.info("Restoring session from bytes, length: " + data.length);
    if (data.length == 0) return null;
    // Уязвимость: Опасная десериализация
    ObjectInputStream ois = new ObjectInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(data));
    Object obj = ois.readObject();
    Logger.debug("Session object restored: " + obj.getClass().getName());
    return obj;
}|||LABEL|||5

public Object deepCopy(Object oldObj) throws Exception {
    Logger.debug("Creating deep copy via serialization");
    ByteArrayOutputStream baos = new ByteArrayOutputStream();
    new ObjectOutputStream(baos).writeObject(oldObj);
    ByteArrayInputStream bais = new ByteArrayInputStream(baos.toByteArray());
    // Уязвимость: Даже внутренний deep copy через десериализацию опасен
    return new ObjectInputStream(bais).readObject();
}|||LABEL|||5

public void processByteObject(byte[] data) throws Exception {
    if (data.length < 10) return;
    Logger.info("Decoding ObjectInputStream...");
    ObjectInputStream ois = new ObjectInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(data));
    // Уязвимость: Десериализация
    ois.readObject();

public User findUserByAuth(Connection conn, String login, String pass) throws SQLException {
    Logger.info("Authenticating user: " + login);
    Statement st = conn.createStatement();
    // Уязвимость: Конкатенация пароля и логина прямо в строку
    String sql = "SELECT * FROM users WHERE login = '" + login + "' AND password = '" + pass + "'";
    Logger.debug("Executing query: " + sql);
    ResultSet rs = st.executeQuery(sql);
    if (rs.next()) {
        return new User(rs.getInt("id"), rs.getString("name"));
    }
    return null;

public List<Product> searchProducts(String category, String query) throws SQLException {
    System.out.println("Search request: cat=" + category + ", q=" + query);
    Statement st = connection.createStatement();
    // Уязвимость: Небезопасная фильтрация
    String sql = "SELECT * FROM products WHERE category = '" + category + "' AND title LIKE '%" + query + "%'";
    ResultSet rs = st.executeQuery(sql);
    List<Product> results = new ArrayList<>();
    while(rs.next()) {
        results.add(new Product(rs.getString("title")));
    }
    return results;

    Statement st = connection.createStatement();
    // Уязвимость: Простой обход кавычки в номере счета
    String sql = "SELECT balance FROM accounts WHERE acc_num = '" + accountNumber + "'";

    return rs.next() ? rs.getDouble(1) : 0.0;

public void forceStopTask(Thread taskThread) {
    Logger.warn("Emergency task termination requested.");
    if (taskThread != null && taskThread.isAlive()) {
        System.out.println("Stopping thread: " + taskThread.getName());
        // Уязвимость: Опасный метод stop()
        taskThread.stop();
        Logger.info("Thread has been signaled to stop.");
    }

public void updateStatusSecure(String id, String status) {
    Logger.info("Updating status for: " + id);
    // Безопасно: использование параметров в JdbcTemplate (аргументы передаются отдельно)
    jdbcTemplate.update("UPDATE orders SET status = ? WHERE uuid = ?", status, id);
    System.out.println("Update queued successfully");
}|||LABEL|||0

public String readDataCorrectly(Path p) throws IOException {
    Logger.debug("Opening file for reading...");
    // Безопасно: try-with-resources закроет поток автоматически
    try (InputStream is = Files.newInputStream(p)) {
        byte[] buffer = new byte[is.available()];
        is.read(buffer);
        return new String(buffer);
    }
}|||LABEL|||0

public void handleCalculation(String input) {
    try {
        int result = Integer.parseInt(input) * 10;
        Logger.info("Result: " + result);
    } catch (NumberFormatException e) {
        // Безопасно: ошибка не "проглочена", а залогирована с исключением
        Logger.error("Failed to parse input: " + input, e);
        throw new RuntimeException("Invalid data format", e);
    }
}|||LABEL|||0

public Document getXmlStructure(String xml) throws Exception {
    DocumentBuilderFactory dbf = DocumentBuilderFactory.newInstance();
    // Безопасно: DTD отключен, защита от XXE
    dbf.setFeature("http://apache.org/xml/features/disallow-doctype-decl", true);
    DocumentBuilder db = dbf.newDocumentBuilder();
    return db.parse(new InputSource(new StringReader(xml)));
}|||LABEL|||0

public Object lookupServiceSafe() throws Exception {
    Logger.debug("Accessing local JNDI context");
    InitialContext ctx = new InitialContext();
    // Безопасно: используется константная строка, а не ввод пользователя
    return ctx.lookup("java:comp/env/jdbc/DefaultDB");
}|||LABEL|||0

public double calculateDiscountSafe(double price) {
    Logger.trace("Calculating discount...");
    if (price > 1000) {
        return price * 0.9;
    }
    return price;
}|||LABEL|||0
